@OptIn(SymbolInternals::class)\n507\t    private fun FirClassSymbol<*>.createEmptyBuilderClass(\n508\t        session: FirSession,\n509\t        name: Name,\n510\t        visibility: `@Builder`:\n562\t     *\n563\t     * ```kt\n564\t     * @lombok.Builder\n565\t     * public class C<T> {\n566\t     *     private final T value;\n567\t     * }\n568\t     * ```\n569\t     *\n570\t     * That has the following generated builder:\n571\t     *\n572\t     * ```kt\n573\t     * import lombok.Generated;\n574\t     *\n575\t     * public class C<T> {\n576\t     *     private final T     *         @Generated\n604\t     *         public C<T> build() {\n605\t     *             return new C<T>(this.value);\n606\t     *         }\n607\t     *\n608\t     *         @Generated\n609\t     *         public String toString() {\n610\t     *             return \"C.CBuilder(value=\" + String.valueOf(this.value) + \")\";\n611\t     *         }\n612\t     *     }\n613\t     * }\n614\t     * ```\n615\t     *\n616\t     * We have to initialize the new type parameters for static `builder` (T -> T2) to make Java resolve robust:\n617\t     *\n618\t     * ```kt\n619\t     * public static <T2> T3);\n625\t     *\n626\t     * ```kt\n627\t     * public static class CBuilder<T3> {\n628\t     *     ...\n629\t     *     @Generated\n630\t     *     public CBuilder<T3> value(T3 value) {\n631\t     *         this.value = value;\n632\t     *         return this;\n633\t     *     }\n634\t     *     @Generated\n635\t     *     public C<T3> build() {\n636\t     *         return new */\n644\t    @OptIn(SymbolInternals::class)\n645\t    private fun FirDeclaration.initializeTypeParametersMapping(newContainingDeclarationSymbol: FirBasedSymbol<*>): Map<JavaTypeParameter, FirTypeParameter> {\n646\t        val typeParameters: List<FirTypeParameter> = when (this) {\n647\t            is FirJavaClass -> typeParameters.map { it.symbol.fir }\n648\t            is FirJavaMethod -> typeParameters\n649\t            is FirJavaConstructor -> typeParameters.map { it.symbol.fir }\n650\t            else -> emptyList() // Use the fallback just in case, although it's normally unreachable\n651\t        }\n652\t        return buildMap {\n653\t            for (typeParameter in typeParameters) {\n654\t                // Normally it's always `FirJavaTypeParameter` but newContainingDeclarationSymbol\n660\t                }\n661\t            }\n662\t        }\n663\t    }\n664\t\n665\t    private fun T.getBuilderClassShortName(builderDeclaration: FirDeclaration):           is FirJavaClass -> builderDeclaration.name.asString()\n672\t            is FirJavaConstructor -> builderDeclaration.nameOrSpecialName.asString()\n673\t            is FirJavaMethod -> FirJavaTypeRef)?.type) {\n677\t                    is JavaPrimitiveType -> returnType.type?.typeName?.identifier ?: \"Void\"\n678\t                    is JavaClassifierType -> WithGenerator(session: FirSession) : FirDeclarationGenerationExtension(session) {\n    private val lombokService: LombokService\n        get() = session.lombokService\n\n    private val cache: FirCache<FirClassSymbol<*>, Map<Name, FirJavaMethod>?, Nothing?> =\n        session.firCachesFactory.createCache(::createWith)\n\n    override fun getCallableNamesForClass(classSymbol: FirClassSymbol<*>, context: MemberGenerationContext): Set<Name> {\n        if (!classSymbol.isSuitableJavaClass()) return emptySet()\n        return cache.getValue(classSymbol)?.keys ?: emptySet()\n    }\n\n    override fun generateFunctions(callableId: CallableId, context: MemberGenerationContext?): List<FirNamedFunctionSymbol> {\n        val owner = context?.owner\n        if (owner == null || !owner.isSuitableJavaClass()) return emptyList()\n        val getter = cache.getValue(owner)?.get(callableId.callableName) ?: return emptyList()\n        return listOf(getter.symbol)\n    }\n\n    private fun createWith(classSymbol: FirClassSymbol<*>): Map<Name, FirJavaMethod>? {\n        val nonStaticFieldsWithWith = computeNonStaticFieldsWithWithAnnotation(classSymbol) ?: return null\n        return nonStaticFieldsWithWith.mapNotNull { (field, withInfo) ->\n            val withName = computeWithName(field, withInfo) ?: return@mapNotNull null\n\n            val function = classSymbol.createJavaMethod(\n                name = withName,\n                valueParameters = listOf(ConeLombokValueParameter(field.name, field.returnTypeRef)),\n                returnTypeRef = buildResolvedTypeRef {\n                    coneType = classSymbol.defaultType()\n                },\n                visibility = withInfo.visibility.toVisibility(),\n                modality = Modality.OPEN,\n            )\n\n            withName to function\n        }.toMap()\n    }\n\n    @OptIn(SymbolInternals::class)\n    private fun computeNonStaticFieldsWithWithAnnotation(classSymbol: FirClassSymbol<*>): List<Pair<FirJavaField, With>>? {\n        val classWith = lombokService.getWith(classSymbol)\n\n        return classSymbol.fir.declarations\n            .filterIsInstance<FirJavaField>()\n            .filter { !it.isStatic }\n            .collectWithNotNull { lombokService.getWith(it.symbol) ?: classWith }\n            .takeIf { it.isNotEmpty() }\n    }\n\n    private fun computeWithName(field: FirJavaField, withInfo: With): Name? {\n        if (withInfo.visibility == AccessLevel.NONE) return null\n        val functionName = \"with\" + field.name.identifier.normalizeAndCapitalize(field.returnTypeRef.isPrimitiveBoolean())\n        return Name.identifier(functionName)\n    }\n}\n```"}]},"uuid":"10293f8d-c2bd-4ac1-9cab-320f7b96d366","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:18:46.073Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"5b29c55b-8068-4ba6-b9d4-87cf0ccdaeb5","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

LombokService Class Overview\n\nThis Kotlin file defines a `LombokService` class that manages Lombok annotation configurations within the Kotlin compiler's FIR (Frontend Intermediate Representation) framework.\n\n## Key Components\n\n**Purpose**: The service provides cached access to various Lombok annotation metadata for FIR symbols, enabling the compiler to process Lombok-generated code during analysis.\n\n**Core Functionality**:\n- Initializes with a FIR session and optional configuration file\n- Parses Lombok configuration via `LombokConfig.parse()`\n- Maintains multiple caches for different annotation types\n\n**Supported Annotations** (via dedicated caches):\nAccessors, Getter, Setter, With, NoArgsConstructor, AllArgsConstructor, RequiredArgsConstructor, Data, Value, Builder, SuperBuilder, and Singular\n\n**Access Pattern**: Each annotation type has a corresponding getter method (e.g., `getAccessors()`, `getGetter()`) that retrieves cached results without recomputation.\n\n**Registration**: The service integrates with FIR's extension system through `FirExtensionSessionComponent` and registers via a session property accessor named `lombokService`.\n\n**Technical Notes**: Uses `@OptIn(SymbolInternals::class)` to access internal compiler APIs, suggesting this is part of Kotlin's official compiler infrastructure rather than a plugin."}]},"uuid":"b3602c82-4098-4ec3-bee3-b413b869f501","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:18:46.082Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"0b9df2b4-82eb-4fb3-a069-3153473cce82","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

     val (classSymbol, declaredScope) = key\n        val data = lombokService.getData(classSymbol)\n        val fieldsWithAccessor = computeFieldsWithAccessors(classSymbol, data) ?: return null\n        val globalAccessors = lombokService.getAccessors(classSymbol)\n        val explicitlyDeclaredFunctions = declaredScope?.collectAllFunctions()?.associateBy { it.name }.orEmpty()\n        return buildMap {\n            fieldsWithAccessor.forEach { (field, getter, setter) ->\n                val dispatchReceiverType = runIf(!field.isStatic) { classSymbol.defaultType() }\n                val     name = getterName,\n                        valueParameters = emptyList(),\n                        returnTypeRef = field.returnTypeRef,\n                        visibility = field.isStatic,\n                    )\n\n                    getOrPut(getterName) { mutableListOf() }.add(function)\n                }\n\n                val setterName = setter?.let { session.builtinTypes.unitType\n                    }\n\n                    val function = classSymbol.createJavaMethod(\n                        name = setterName,\n                        valueParameters = listOf(ConeLombokValueParameter(field.name, field.returnTypeRef)),\n                        returnTypeRef = returnTypeRef,\n                        visibility = setter.visibility.toVisibility(),\n                        modality = Modality.OPEN,\n                        dispatchReceiverType = dispatchReceiverType,\n                        isStatic = field.isStatic,\n                    )\n\n                    getOrPut(setterName) { mutableListOf() }.add(function)\n                }\n            }\n\n            if (data != null) {\n runIf(!declaration.isStatic) { classSetter }\n                }\n\n                if (getter != null || setter != null) {\n                    add(FieldWithAccessors(declaration, getter, setter))\n                }\n            }\n        }.takeIf { it.isNotEmpty() }\n    }\n\n    private fun computeAccessorName(\n        field: FirJavaField,\n        accessorInfo: ConeLombokAnnotations.AbstractAccessor,\n        localAccessors: Accessors?,\n        globalAccessors: Accessors,\n    ): Name? {\n        if (accessorInfo.visibility == AccessLevel.NONE) return null\n\n        val prefixes = localAccessors?.prefix ?: globalAccessors.prefix ?: emptyList()\n        // Don't generate the accessor if the field doesn't match any provided prefix\n        val propertyName = field.extractPropertyNameOrNull(prefixes) ?: return null\n\n        val isPrimitiveBoolean = field.returnTypeRef.isPrimitiveBoolean()\n        val functionName = if (localAccessors?.fluent ?: globalAccessors.fluent ?: false) {\n            propertyName\n        } else {\n            val prefix = when (accessorInfo) {\n                is Getter -> {\n                    if (isPrimitiveBoolean && !globalAccessors.noIsPrefix)\n                        AccessorNames.IS\n                    else\n                        AccessorNames.GET\n                }\n                is Setter -> {\n                    AccessorNames.SET\n                }\n            }\n\n            prefix + propertyName.normalizeAndCapitalize(isPrimitiveBoolean)\n        }\n        return Name.identifier(functionName)\n    }\n\n    private fun FirJavaField.extractPropertyNameOrNull(prefixes: List<String>): String? {\n        val fieldId = name.identifier\n        if (prefixes.isEmpty()) {\n            return fieldId\n        }\n\n        return prefixes.firstNotNullOfOrNull {\n            if (it.isEmpty()) {\n                return@firstNotNullOfOrNull fieldId\n CliOptionProcessingException(\"Unknown option: ${option.optionName}\")\n380\t    }\n381\t}\n382\t\n383\t/**\n384\t * A list of features that can be enabled through the \"featureFlags\" option.\n385\t *\n386\t * Features should be added to this list if they are intended to eventually become the default\n387\t * behavior of the compiler. This is intended to allow progressive roll-out of a feature to\n388\t * facilitate coordinating the runtime and compiler changes. New features should be disabled\n389\t * by default until it is validated to be ready for production after testing with the corresponding\n390\t * changes needed in the runtime. Using this technique does not remove the need to feature detect\n391\t * for the version of runtime and is only intended to disable the feature even if the feature is\n392\t * detected in the runtime.\n393\t *\n394\t * If a feature default is `true` the feature is reported as known by the command-line processor\n395\t * but will generate a warning that the option is no longer necessary as it is the default. If\n396\t * the feature is not in this list a warning is produced instead of an error to facilitate moving\n397\t * compiler versions without having to always remove features unknown to older versions of the\n398\t * plugin.\n399\t *\n400\t * A feature flag enum value can be used in the transformers that derive from\n401\t * AbstractComposeLowering by using the FeatureFlag.enabled extension property. For example\n402\t * testing if StrongSkipping is enabled can be checked by checking\n403\t *\n404\t *    FeatureFlag.StrongSkipping.enabled\n405\t *\n406\t * The `default` field is the source of truth for the default of the property. Turning it\n407\t * to `true` here will make it default on even if the value was previous enabled through\n408\t * a deprecated explicit option.\n409\t *\n410\t * A feature can be explicitly disabled by prefixing the feature name with \"-\" even if\n411\t * the feature is enabled by default.\n412\t *\n413\t * @param featureName The name of the feature that is used with featureFlags to enable or disable\n414\t *   the feature.\n415\t * @param default True if the feature is enabled by default or false if it is not.\n416\t */\n417\tenum class FeatureFlag(val featureName: String, val default: Boolean) {\n418\t    StrongSkipping(\"StrongSkipping\", default = true),\n419\t    IntrinsicRemember(\"IntrinsicRemember\", default = true),\n420\t    OptimizeNonSkippingGroups(\"OptimizeNonSkippingGroups\", default = true),\n421\t    PausableComposition(\"PausableComposition\", default = true),\n422\t    ;\n423\t\n424\t    val disabledName get() = \"-$featureName\"\n425\t    fun name(enabled: Boolean) = if (enabled) featureName else disabledName\n426\t\n427\t    companion object {\n428\t        fun fromString(featureName: String): Pair<FeatureFlag?, Boolean> {\n429\t            val (featureToSearch, enabled) = when {\n430\t                featureName.startsWith(\"+\") -> featureName.substring(1) to true\n431\t                featureName.startsWith(\"-\") -> featureName.substring(1) to false\n432\t                else -> featureName to true\n433\t            }\n434\t            return FeatureFlag.entries.firstOrNull {\n435\t                featureToSearch.trim().equals(it.featureName, ignoreCase = true)\n436\t            } to enabled\n437\t        }\n438\t    }\n439\t}\n440\t\n441\tclass FeatureFlags(featureConfiguration: List<String> = emptyList()) {\n442\t    private val setForCompatibility = mutableSetOf<FeatureFlag>()\n443\t    private val duplicate = mutableSetOf<FeatureFlag>()\n444\t    private val enabledFeatures = mutableSetOf<FeatureFlag>()\n445\t    private val disabledFeatures = mutableSetOf<FeatureFlag>()\n446\t\n447\t    init {\n448\t        processConfigurationList(featureConfiguration)\n449\t    }\n450\t\n451\t    private fun enableFeature(feature: FeatureFlag) {\n452\t        if (feature in disabledFeatures) {\n453\t            duplicate.add(feature)\n454\t            disabledFeatures.remove(feature)\n455\t        }\n456\t        enabledFeatures.add(feature)\n457\t    }\n458\t\n459\t    private fun disableFeature(feature: FeatureFlag) {\n460\t        if (feature in enabledFeatures) {\n461\t            duplicate.add(feature)\n462\t            enabledFeatures.remove(feature)\n463\t        }\n464\t        disabledFeatures.add(feature)\n465\t    }\n466\t\n467\t    fun setFeature(feature: FeatureFlag, value: Boolean) {\n468\t        if (feature.default != value) {\n469\t            setForCompatibility.add(feature)\n470\t            if (value) enableFeature(feature) else disableFeature(feature)\n471\t        }\n472\t    }\n473\t\n474\t    fun isEnabled(feature: FeatureFlag) = feature in enabledFeatures || (feature.default &&\n475\t            feature !in disabledFeatures)\n476\t\n477\t    private fun processConfigurationList(featuresNames: List<String>) {\n478\t        for (featureName in featuresNames) {\n479\t            val (feature, enabled) = FeatureFlag.fromString(featureName)\n480\t            if (feature != null) {\n481\t                if (enabled) enableFeature(feature) else disableFeature(feature)\n482\t            }\n483\t        }\n484\t    }\n485\t\n486\t    fun validateFeatureFlags(configuration: CompilerConfiguration) {\n487\t        val msgCollector = configuration.get(CommonConfigurationKeys.MESSAGE_COLLECTOR_KEY)\n488\t        if (msgCollector != null) {\n489\t            val reported = mutableSetOf<FeatureFlag>()\n490\t            fun report(feature: FeatureFlag, message: String) {\n491\t                if (feature !in reported) {\n492\t                    reported.add(feature)\n493\t                    msgCollector.report(\n494\t                        CompilerMessageSeverity.WARNING,\n495\t                        message\n496\t                    )\n497\t                }\n498\t            }\n499\t\n500\t            val configured = enabledFeatures + disabledFeatures\n501\t            val oldAndNewSet = setForCompatibility.intersect(configured)\n502\t            for (feature in oldAndNewSet) {\n503\t                report(\n504\t                    feature,\n505\t                    \"Feature ${featureFlagName()}=${feature.featureName} is using featureFlags \" +\n506\t                            \"and is set using the deprecated option. It is recommended to only use \" +\n507\t                            \"featureFlag. ${currentState(feature)}\"\n508\t                )\n509\t            }\n510\t            for (feature in duplicate) {\n511\t                if (feature !in reported) {\n512\t                    report(\n513\t                        feature,\n514\t                        \"Feature ${featureFlagName()}=${feature.featureName} was both enabled \" +\n515\t                                \"and disabled. ${currentState(feature)}\"\n516\t                    )\n517\t                }\n518\t            }\n519\t            for (feature in disabledFeatures) {\n520\t                if (!feature.default) {\n521\t                    report(\n522\t                        feature,\n523\t                        \"The feature ${featureFlagName()}=${feature.featureName} is disabled \" +\n524\t                                \"by default and specifying this option explicitly is not necessary.\"\n525\t                    )\n526\t                }\n527\t            }\n528\t            for (feature in enabledFeatures) {\n529\t                if (feature.default) {\n530\t                    report(\n531\t                        feature,\n532\t                        \"The feature ${featureFlagName()}=${feature.featureName} is enabled \" +\n533\t                                \"by default and specifying this option explicitly is not necessary.\"\n534\t                    )\n535\t                }\n536\t            }\n537\t        }\n538\t    }\n539\t\n540\t        }\"\n544\t}\n545\t\n546\tfun featureFlagName() =\n547\t    \"plugin:${COMPOSE_PLUGIN_ID}:${\n548\t        ComposeCommandLineProcessor.FEATURE_FLAG_OPTION.optionName\n549\t    }\"\n550\t\n551\tfun useFeatureFlagInsteadMessage(feature: FeatureFlag) = \"Use \" +\n552\t        \"${featureFlagName()}=${feature.featureName} instead\"\n553\t\n554\tfun   }\n53\t}\n54\t\n55\t// Serialize composable function types as normal function types with the\n56\t// @Composable annotation instead of using K2 specific metadata for custom\n57\t// function types. This is to allow the K1 compose compiler plugin\n58\t// to understand libraries produced with the K2 compose compiler plugin.\n59\t//\n60\t// We use the latest value in the LanguageVersion enum to make sure that\n61\t// we do not have to hardcode a version here and have control over when\n62\t// we start using the K2 only serialization format. androidx.compose.compiler.plugins.kotlin.ComposeCallableIds\n20\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.KtSourceElement\n21\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.diagnostics.DiagnosticReporter\n22\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.diagnostics.reportOn\n23\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.FirElement\n24\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.analysis.checkers.MppCheckerKind\n25\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.analysis.checkers.context.CheckerContext\n26\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.analysis.checkers.expression.FirFunctionCallChecker\n27\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.analysis.checkers.expression.FirPropertyAccessExpressionChecker\n28\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.declarations.*\n29\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.declarations.utils.isInline\n30\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.expressions.*\n31\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.expressions.impl.FirResolvedArgumentList\n32\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.references.toResolvedCallableSymbol\n33\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.references.toResolvedFunctionSymbol\n34\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.references.toResolvedValueParameterSymbol\n35\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.resolve.isInvoke\n36\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.symbols.impl.FirCallableSymbol\n37\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.symbols.impl.FirRegularPropertySymbol\n38\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.types.coneType\n39\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.fir.types.functionTypeKind\n40\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.name.CallableId\n41\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.name.FqName\n42\timport org.jetbrains.kotlin.name.Name\n43\t\n44\tobject ComposablePropertyAccessExpressionChecker : FirPropertyAccessExpressionChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common) {\n45\t    context(context: CheckerContext, reporter: DiagnosticReporter)\n46\t    override fun check(expression: FirPropertyAccessExpression) {\n47\t        val calleeFunction = expression.calleeReference.toResolvedCallableSymbol()\n48\t            ?: return\n49\t        if (calleeFunction.isComposable(context.session)) {\n50\t            checkComposableCall(expression, calleeFunction, context, reporter)\n51\t        }\n52\t    }\n53\t}\n54\t\n55\tobject ComposableFunctionCallChecker : FirFunctionCallChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common) {\n56\t    context(context: CheckerContext, reporter: DiagnosticReporter)\n57\t    override fun check(expression: FirFunctionCall) {\n58\t        val calleeFunction = expression.calleeReference.toResolvedFunctionSymbol()\n59\t            ?: return\n60\t\n61\t        // K2 propagates annotation from the fun interface method to the constructor.\n62\t        // https://youtrack.jetbrains.com/issue/KT-47708.\n63\t        if (calleeFunction.origin == FirDeclarationOrigin.SamConstructor) return\n64\t\n65\t        if (calleeFunction.isComposable(context.session)) {\n66\t            checkComposableCall(expression, calleeFunction, context, reporter)\n67\t        } else if (calleeFunction.callableId.isInvoke()) {\n68\t            checkInvoke(expression, context, reporter)\n69\t        }\n70\t    }\n71\t}\n72\t\n73\tprivate val runCatchingCallableId = CallableId(\n74\t    FqName(\"kotlin\"),\n75\t    Name.identifier(\"runCatching\"),\n76\t);\n77\t\n78\t/**\n79\t * Check if `expression` - a call to a composable function or access to a composable property -\n80\t * is allowed in the current context. It is allowed if:\n81\t *\n82\t * - It is executed as part of the body of a composable function.\n83\t * - It is not executed as part of the body of a lambda annotated with `@DisallowComposableCalls`.\n84\t * - It is not inside of a `try` block.\n85\t * - It is not inside of the body of a lambda passed to a `runCatching` call. (As for references to\n86\t *   `@Composable` functions, the type system prevents those from being passed to `runCatching`\n87\t *   calls.)\n88\t * - It is a call to a readonly composable function if it is executed in the body of a function\n89\t *   that is annotated with `@ReadOnlyComposable`.\n90\t *\n91\t * A function is composable if:\n92\t * - It is annotated with `@Composable`.\n93\t * - It is a lambda whose type is inferred to be `ComposableFunction`.\n94\t * - It is an inline lambda whose enclosing function is composable.\n95\t */\n96\tprivate fun checkComposableCall(\n97\t    expression: FirQualifiedAccessExpression,\n98\t    calleeFunction: FirCallableSymbol<*>,\n99\t    context: CheckerContext,\n100\t    reporter: DiagnosticReporter,\n101\t) {\n102\t    if (calleeFunction.callableId == ComposeCallableIds.key) {\n103\t        // If key call only has the block argument, report it\n104\t        if (expression is FirFunctionCall && expression.arguments.size == 1) {\n105\t            reporter.reportOn(\n106\t                expression.calleeReference.source,\n107\t                ComposeErrors.KEY_CALL_WITH_NO_ARGUMENTS,\n108\t                context\n109\t            )\n110\t        }\n111\t    }\n112\t\n113\t    context.visitCurrentScope(\n114\t        visitInlineLambdaParameter = { parameter ->\n115\t            val containingDeclarationSymbol = parameter.containingDeclarationSymbol\n116\t            if (parameter.returnTypeRef.hasDisallowComposableCallsAnnotation(context.session) && containingDeclarationSymbol is FirCallableSymbol) {\n117\t                reporter.reportOn(\n118\t                    expression.calleeReference.source,\n119\t                    ComposeErrors.CAPTURED_COMPOSABLE_INVOCATION,\n120\t                    parameter.symbol,\n121\t                    containingDeclarationSymbol,\n122\t                    context\n123\t                )\n124\t            }\n125\t        },\n126\t        visitAnonymousFunction = { function ->\n127\t            if (function.typeRef.coneType.functionTypeKind(context.session) === ComposableFunction)\n128\t                return\n129\t            if (function.isLambda) {\n130\t                return@visitCurrentScope\n131\t            }\n132\t            val nonReadOnlyCalleeReference =\n133\t                if (!calleeFunction.isReadOnlyComposable(context.session)) {\n134\t                    expression.calleeReference.source\n135\t                } else {\n136\t                    null\n137\t                }\n138\t            if (checkComposableFunction(\n139\t                    function,\n140\t                    nonReadOnlyCalleeReference,\n141\t                    context,\n142\t                    reporter,\n143\t                ) == ComposableCheckForScopeStatus.STOP\n144\t            ) {\n145\t                return\n146\t            }\n147\t        },\n148\t        visitFunction = { function ->\n149\t            val nonReadOnlyCalleeReference =\n150\t                if (!calleeFunction.isReadOnlyComposable(context.session)) {\n151\t                    expression.calleeReference.source\n152\t                } else {\n153\t                    null\n154\t                }\n155\t            if (checkComposableFunction(\n156\t                    function,\n157\t                    nonReadOnlyCalleeReference,\n158\t                    context,\n159\t                    reporter,\n160\t                ) == ComposableCheckForScopeStatus.STOP\n161\t            ) {\n162\t                return\n163\t            }\n164\t        },\n165\t        visitTryExpression = { tryExpression, container ->\n166\t            // Only report an error if the composable call happens inside of the `try`\n167\t            // block. Composable calls are allowed inside of `catch` and `finally` blocks.\n168\t            if (container !is FirCatch && tryExpression.finallyBlock != container) {\n169\t                reporter.reportOn(\n170\t                    tryExpression.source,\n171\t                    ComposeErrors.ILLEGAL_TRY_CATCH_AROUND_COMPOSABLE,\n172\t                    context\n173\t                )\n174\t            }\n175\t        },\n176\t        visitFunctionCall = { functionCall ->\n177\t            if (functionCall.calleeReference.toResolvedCallableSymbol()?.callableId == runCatchingCallableId) {\n178\t                // If we have reached this point, it means that the composable call under scrutiny\n179\t                // happens inside of the body of a lambda passed to a `runCatching` call.\n180\t                reporter.reportOn(\n181\t                    functionCall.source,\n182\t                    ComposeErrors.ILLEGAL_RUN_CATCHING_AROUND_COMPOSABLE,\n183\t                    context\n184\t                )\n185\t            }\n186\t        }\n187\t    )\n188\t    reporter.reportOn(\n189\t        expression.calleeReference.source,\n190\t        ComposeErrors.COMPOSABLE_INVOCATION,\n191\t        context\n192\t    )\n193\t}\n194\t\n195\tprivate enum class ComposableCheckForScopeStatus {\n196\t    STOP,\n197\t    CONTINUE,\n198\t}\n199\t\n200\t/**\n201\t * This function will be called by [visitCurrentScope], and this function determines\n202\t * whether it will continue the composable element check for the scope or not\n203\t * by returning [ComposableCheckForScopeStatus].\n204\t */\n205\tprivate fun checkComposableFunction(\n206\t    function: FirFunction,\n207\t    nonReadOnlyCallInsideFunction: KtSourceElement?,\n208\t    context: CheckerContext,\n209\t    reporter: DiagnosticReporter,\n210\t): ComposableCheckForScopeStatus {\n211\t    // [function] is a function with \"read-only\" composable annotation, but it has a call\n212\t    // without \"read-only\" composable annotation.\n213\t    // -> report NONREADONLY_CALL_IN_READONLY_COMPOSABLE.\n214\t    if (function.hasComposableAnnotation(context.session)) {\n215\t        if (\n216\t            function.hasReadOnlyComposableAnnotation(context.session) &&\n217\t            nonReadOnlyCallInsideFunction != null\n218\t        ) {\n219\t            reporter.reportOn(\n220\t                nonReadOnlyCallInsideFunction,\n221\t                ComposeErrors.NONREADONLY_CALL_IN_READONLY_COMPOSABLE,\n222\t                context\n223\t            )\n224\t        }\n225\t        return ComposableCheckForScopeStatus.STOP\n226\t    }\n227\t    // We allow composable calls in local delegated properties.\n228\t    // The only call this could be is a getValue/setValue in the synthesized getter/setter.\n229\t    if (function is FirPropertyAccessor && function.propertySymbol.hasDelegate) {\n230\t        if (function.propertySymbol.isVar) {\n231\t            reporter.reportOn(\n232\t                function.source,\n233\t                ComposeErrors.COMPOSE_INVALID_DELEGATE,\n234\t                context\n235\t            )\n236\t        }\n237\t        // Only local variables can be implicitly composable, for top-level or class-level\n238\t        // declarations we require an explicit annotation.\n239\t        if (function.propertySymbol is FirRegularPropertySymbol) {\n240\t            reporter.reportOn(\n241\t                function.propertySymbol.source,\n242\t                ComposeErrors.COMPOSABLE_EXPECTED,\n243\t                context\n244\t            )\n245\t        }\n246\t        return ComposableCheckForScopeStatus.STOP\n247\t    }\n248\t    // We've found a non-composable function which contains a composable call.\n249\t    val source = if (function is FirPropertyAccessor) {\n250\t        function.propertySymbol.source\n251\t    } else {\n252\t        function.source\n253\t    }\n254\t    reporter.reportOn(source, ComposeErrors.COMPOSABLE_EXPECTED, context)\n255\t    return ComposableCheckForScopeStatus.CONTINUE\n256\t}\n257\t\n258\t/**\n259\t * Reports an error if we are invoking a lambda parameter of an inline function in a context\n260\t * where composable calls are not allowed, unless the lambda parameter is itself annotated\n261\t * with `@DisallowComposableCalls`.\n262\t */\n263\tprivate fun checkInvoke(\n264\t    expression: FirQualifiedAccessExpression,\n265\t    context: CheckerContext,\n266\t    reporter: DiagnosticReporter,\n267\t) {\n268\t    // Check that we're invoking a value parameter of an inline function\n269\t    val param = (expression.dispatchReceiver as? FirPropertyAccessExpression)\n270\t        ?.calleeReference\n271\t        ?.toResolvedValueParameterSymbol()\n272\t        ?: return\n273\t    if (param.resolvedReturnTypeRef.hasDisallowComposableCallsAnnotation(context.session) ||\n274\t        !param.containingDeclarationSymbol.let { it is FirCallableSymbol && it.isInline }\n275\t    ) {\n276\t        return\n277\t    }\n278\t\n279\t    context.visitCurrentScope(\n280\t        visitInlineLambdaParameter = { parameter ->\n281\t            if (parameter.returnTypeRef.hasDisallowComposableCallsAnnotation(context.session)) {\n282\t                reporter.reportOn(\n283\t                    param.source,\n284\t                    ComposeErrors.MISSING_DISALLOW_COMPOSABLE_CALLS_ANNOTATION,\n285\t                    param,\n286\t                    parameter.symbol,\n287\t                    parameter.containingDeclarationSymbol as FirCallableSymbol,\n288\t                    context\n289\t                )\n290\t            }\n291\t        }\n292\t    )\n293\t}\n294\t\n295\t/**\n296\t * Visits all (Anonymous)Functions and `try` expressions in the current scope until it finds\n297\t * a declaration that introduces a new scope. Elements are visited from innermost to outermost.\n298\t */\n299\tprivate inline fun CheckerContext.visitCurrentScope(\n300\t    visitInlineLambdaParameter: (FirValueParameter) -> Unit,\n301\t    visitAnonymousFunction: (FirAnonymousFunction) -> Unit = {},\n302\t    visitFunction: (FirFunction) -> Unit = {},\n303\t    visitTryExpression: (FirTryExpression, FirElement) -> Unit = { _, _ -> },\n304\t    visitFunctionCall: (FirFunctionCall) -> Unit = {},\n305\t) {\n306\t    for ((elementIndex, element) in containingElements.withIndex().reversed()) {\n307\t        when (element) {\n308\t            is FirAnonymousFunction -> {\n309\t                if (element.inlineStatus == InlineStatus.Inline) {\n310\t                    findValueParameterForLambdaAtIndex(elementIndex)?.let { parameter ->\n311\t                        visitInlineLambdaParameter(parameter)\n312\t                    }\n313\t                }\n314\t                visitAnonymousFunction(element)\n315\t                if (element.inlineStatus != InlineStatus.Inline) {\n316\t                    return\n317\t                }\n318\t            }\n319\t            is FirFunction -> {\n320\t                visitFunction(element)\n321\t                return\n322\t            }\n323\t            is FirTryExpression -> {\n324\t                val container = containingElements.getOrNull(elementIndex + 1)\n325\t                    ?: continue\n326\t                visitTryExpression(element, container)\n327\t            }\n328\t            is FirFunctionCall -> {\n329\t                visitFunctionCall(element)\n330\t            }\n331\t            is FirProperty -> {\n332\t                // Coming from an initializer or delegate expression, otherwise we'd\n333\t                // have hit a FirFunction and would already report an error.\n334\t            }\n335\t            is FirValueParameter -> {\n336\t                // We're coming from a default value in a function declaration, we need to\n337\t                // look at the enclosing function.\n338\t            }\n339\t            is FirAnonymousObject, is FirAnonymousInitializer -> {\n340\t                // Anonymous objects don't change the current scope, continue.\n341\t            }\n342\t            is FirField -> {\n343\t                if (element.origin == FirDeclarationOrigin.Synthetic.DelegateField) {\n344\t                    // Delegating in constructor creates a synthetic field in FIR.\n345\t                    // Continue through in this case in case it is an anonymous declaration.\n346\t                } else {\n347\t                    // Other fields introduce new scope which cannot be composable.\n348\t                    return\n349\t                }\n350\t            }\n351\t            // Every other declaration introduces a new scope which cannot be composable.\n352\t            is FirDeclaration -> return\n353\t        }\n354\t    }\n355\t}\n356\t\n357\tprivate fun CheckerContext.findValueParameterForLambdaAtIndex(\n358\t    elementIndex: Int,\n359\t): FirValueParameter? {\n360\t    val function = containingElements.getOrNull(elementIndex) as? FirAnonymousFunction ?: return null\n361\t    val argumentList = containingElements.getOrNull(elementIndex - 1) as? FirResolvedArgumentList ?: return null\n362\t    val argument = argumentList.arguments.find { it is FirAnonymousFunctionExpression && it.anonymousFunction == function } ?: return null\n363\t    return argumentList.mapping[argument]\n364\t}\n365\t"}]},"uuid":"3a403b34-6f8f-47f3-bff1-192c9738209d","timestamp":"2026-04-04T01:19:18.841Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"cbf2fb57-3342-411c-b734-432576919aed","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/tbsten/dev/compose-preview-lab","sessionId":"bf73b4a8-7271-43d1-8dc0-215de078a5e2","version":"2.1.91","gitBranch":"feature/compiler-plugin","slug":"zazzy-swimming-allen"}

every function in the module.\n53\t * In this case \"durable\" means that when the code is edited over time, a function with the same\n54\t * semantic identity will usually have the same key each time it is compiled. This is important so\n55\t * that new code can be recompiled and the key that the function gets after that recompile ought to\n56\t * be the same as before, so one could inject this new code and signal to the runtime that\n57\t * composable functions with that key should be considered invalid.\n58\t *\n59\t * This transform runs early on in the lowering pipeline, and stores the keys for every function in\n60\t * the file in the BindingTrace for each function. Source code url |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| lombok | AccessorGenerator (getter/setter 生成) | FIR | K2 | `plugins/lombok/lombok.k2/src/.../generators/AccessorGenerator.kt` |\n| lombok | WithGenerator |\n| lombok | ValueFieldModifier | - (K1 resolve) | K1 | `plugins/lombok/lombok.k1/src/.../processor/ValueFieldModifier.kt` |\n\n### 各機能の詳細 (K2 FIR Extensions)\n\n##### AccessorGenerator\n- **継承/実装**: `FirDeclarationGenerationExtension(session)`\n- **オーバーライドメソッド**: `getCallableNamesForClass`, `generateFunctions`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - Java ソースクラスのフィールドに対して、`@Getter` / `@Setter` / `@Data` / `@Value` アノテーションに基づいて getter/setter メソッドを合成する\n  - getter 名: boolean フィールドなら `isXxx`、それ以外は `getXxx` (fluent モードなら prefix なし)\n  - setter 名: `setXxx` (fluent/chain モードなら `this` を返す)\n  - `@Accessors` の `prefix`, `fluent`, `chain`, `noIsPrefix` 設定を考慮\n  - `@Data` アノテーション付きクラスには `canEqual(Object)` メソッドも生成\n  - 既にクラスに同名メソッドがある場合はスキップ (名前のみで判定、パラメータ数は無視)\n- **診断メッセージ**: なし (生成のみ)\n\n##### WithGenerator\n- **継承/実装**: `FirDeclarationGenerationExtension(session)`\n- **オーバーライドメソッド**: `getCallableNamesForClass`, `generateFunctions`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - `@With` アノテーションが付いた Java フィールドに対して `withXxx(value)` メソッドを生成\n  - 返り値はクラス自身の型 (新しいインスタンスを返す immutable パターン)\n  - クラスレベルの `@With` もサポート (全 non-static フィールドに適用)\n  - `AccessLevel.NONE` の場合はスキップ\n\n##### LombokConstructorsGenerator\n- **継承/実装**: `FirDeclarationGenerationExtension(session)`\n- **オーバーライドメソッド**: `getCallableNamesForClass`, `generateFunctions`, `generateConstructors`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - 内部に3つのパートを持つ:\n    1. **AllArgsConstructorGeneratorPart**: `@AllArgsConstructor` (全フィールドを引数に取るコンストラクタ)。`@Builder` や `@Value` からも暗黙的に生成\n    2. **NoArgsConstructorGeneratorPart**: `@NoArgsConstructor` (引数なしコンストラクタ)\n    3. **RequiredArgsConstructorGeneratorPart**: `@RequiredArgsConstructor` (final フィールド + `@NonNull` フィールドのみ)。`@Data` からも暗黙的に生成\n  - `staticName` が指定されている場合、コンストラクタの代わりに static ファクトリメソッドを生成\n  - 衝突する既存コンストラクタがある場合はスキップ (引数数のみで判定)\n\n##### BuilderGenerator\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractBuilderGenerator<Builder>(session)` extends `FirDeclarationGenerationExtension`\n- **オーバーライドメソッド**: `getCallableNamesForClass`, `getNestedClassifiersNames`, `generateFunctions`, `generateNestedClassLikeDeclaration`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - `@Builder` アノテーション付き Java クラス/コンストラクタ/メソッドに対して Builder パターンを生成\n  - 生成するもの:\n    - **ネストクラス**: `XxxBuilder` (modality: FINAL)\n    - **エンティティメソッド**: `builder()` (static), `toBuilder()` (オプション)\n    - **ビルダーメソッド**: フィールドごとの setter、`build()` メソッド\n  - `@Singular` 対応: Collection/Map/Table 型フィールドに対して単数形の追加メソッド + `clearXxx()` を生成\n  - Guava コレクション対応 (`ImmutableList`, `ImmutableMap` 等)\n  - 型パラメータのリマッピング処理あり (ジェネリッククラスの Builder)\n\n##### SuperBuilderGenerator\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractBuilderGenerator<SuperBuilder>(session)` extends `FirDeclarationGenerationExtension`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - `@SuperBuilder` 用。`@Builder` との違いは継承をサポートすること\n  - Builder クラスの modality は **ABSTRACT**\n  - 追加の型パラメータ `C` (エンティティ型) と `B` (ビルダー自身の型) を生成\n  - `self()` (abstract/protected) と `build()` (abstract) メソッドを追加\n  - 親クラスの SuperBuilder を superType として設定\n\n##### DeclarationWithValueAnnStatusTransformer\n- **継承/実装**: `FirStatusTransformerExtension(session)`\n- **オーバーライドメソッド**: `needTransformStatus`, `transformStatus` (FirField 用), `transformStatus` (FirRegularClass 用)\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - `@Value` アノテーション付きクラスの Java フィールドの可視性を `PackageVisibility` -> `Private` に変更\n  - `@Value` アノテーション付きクラスの modality を `FINAL` に変更\n\n##### LombokService\n- **継承/実装**: `FirExtensionSessionComponent(session)`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - lombok.config の解析結果を保持\n  - 各アノテーション (`@Getter`, `@Setter`, `@With`, `@Data`, `@Value`, `@Builder`, `@SuperBuilder`, `@NoArgsConstructor`, `@AllArgsConstructor`, `@RequiredArgsConstructor`, `@Singular`, `@Accessors`) のキャッシュ\n\n### 診断メッセージ (LombokDiagnostics)\n- `LOMBOK_PLUGIN_IS_EXPERIMENTAL` (warning): プラグインが experimental であることの警告\n- `LOMBOK_CONFIG_IS_MISSING` (warning): lombok.config ファイルが見つからない\n- `UNKNOWN_PLUGIN_OPTION` (error): 不明なプラグインオプション\n\n### K1 用 Extension\n\n##### LombokResolveExtension / LombokSyntheticJavaPartsProvider\n- **継承/実装**: `SyntheticJavaResolveExtension` -> `SyntheticJavaPartsProvider`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - K1 では `SyntheticJavaPartsProvider` として、Java クラスにシンセティックメンバーを追加する仕組み\n  - 7つの Processor を持つ: `GetterProcessor`, `SetterProcessor`, `WithProcessor`, `NoArgsConstructorProcessor`, `AllArgsConstructorProcessor`, `RequiredArgsConstructorProcessor`, `BuilderProcessor`\n  - `ValueFieldModifier` でフィールドの modality/visibility を変更\n  - 各 Processor は `Processor` インターフェースの `contribute(ClassDescriptor, SyntheticPartsBuilder, LazyJavaResolverContext)` を実装\n  - 結果は `SyntheticParts` (methods, staticFunctions, constructors, classes) にキャッシュ\n\n---\n\n## Compose プラグイン\n\n### 登録エントリポイント\n\n- **ファイル**: `plugins/compose/compiler-hosted/src/main/java/androidx/compose/compiler/plugins/kotlin/ComposePlugin.kt`\n  - GitHub: https://github.com/JetBrains/kotlin/blob/master/plugins/compose/compiler-hosted/src/main/java/androidx/compose/compiler/plugins/kotlin/ComposePlugin.kt\n- **クラス**: `ComposePluginRegistrar : CompilerPluginRegistrar()`\n- **pluginId**: `androidx.compose.compiler.plugins.kotlin`\n- **supportsK2**: `true`\n- **登録内容** (`registerExtensions`):\n  - **K1 + K2 共通**:\n    - `StorageComponentContainerContributor.registerExtension(ComposableCallChecker())` -- K1\n    - `StorageComponentContainerContributor.registerExtension(ComposableDeclarationChecker())` -- K1\n    - `StorageComponentContainerContributor.registerExtension(ComposableTargetChecker())` -- K1\n    - `StorageComponentContainerContributor.registerExtension(ComposableAnnotationChecker())` -- K1\n    - `DiagnosticSuppressor.registerExtension(ComposeDiagnosticSuppressor())` -- K1\n    - `TypeResolutionInterceptor.registerExtension(ComposeTypeResolutionInterceptorExtension())` -- K1\n    - `DescriptorSerializerPlugin.registerExtension(ClassStabilityFieldSerializationPlugin(...))` -- K1/K2\n    - `FirExtensionRegistrar.registerExtension(ComposeFirExtensionRegistrar())` -- K2\n  - **IR (K1 + K2 共通)**:\n    - `IrGenerationExtension.registerExtension(ComposeIrGenerationExtension(...))` -- IR\n  - **K1 Native のみ**:\n    - `DescriptorSerializerPlugin.registerExtension(AddHiddenFromObjCSerializationPlugin(...))` -- K1\n\n#### ComposeFirExtensionRegistrar (K2 FIR)\n\n- **ファイル**: `plugins/compose/compiler-hosted/src/.../k2/ComposeFirExtensions.kt`\n- **登録内容**:\n  - `+::ComposableFunctionTypeKindExtension` -- FirFunctionTypeKindExtension\n  - `+::ComposeFirCheckersExtension` -- FirAdditionalCheckersExtension\n  - `+::ComposableTargetSessionStorage` -- FirExtensionSessionComponent\n  - `registerDiagnosticContainers(ComposeErrors)`\n\n### 機能一覧テーブル\n\n| プラグイン名 | 実装されている機能 | FIR or IR | K2 or K1 | Source code url |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| compose | ComposableFunctionTypeKindExtension | FIR | K2 | `ComposeFirExtensions.kt` |\n| compose | ComposeFirCheckersExtension | FIR | K2 | `ComposeFirExtensions.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableFunctionChecker | FIR | K2 | `ComposableFunctionChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposablePropertyChecker | FIR | K2 | `ComposablePropertyChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableAnnotationChecker (ResolvedTypeRef) | FIR | K2 | `ComposableAnnotationChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableFunctionCallChecker | FIR | K2 | `ComposableCallChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposablePropertyAccessExpressionChecker | FIR | K2 | `ComposableCallChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposablePropertyReferenceChecker | FIR | K2 | `ComposablePropertyChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableTargetChecker | FIR | K2 | `ComposableTargetChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableTargetSessionStorage | FIR | K2 | `ComposableTargetChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableLambdaAnnotator | IR | K2 | `ComposableLambdaAnnotator.kt` |\n| compose | AddHiddenFromObjCLowering | IR | K2 | `AddHiddenFromObjCLowering.kt` |\n| compose | ClassStabilityTransformer | IR | K1+K2 | `ClassStabilityTransformer.kt` |\n| compose | LiveLiteralTransformer | IR | K1+K2 | `LiveLiteralTransformer.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableFunInterfaceLowering | IR | K1+K2 | `ComposableFunInterfaceLowering.kt` |\n| compose | DurableFunctionKeyTransformer | IR | K1+K2 | `DurableFunctionKeyTransformer.kt` |\n| compose | CopyDefaultValuesFromExpectLowering | IR | K1 only | `CopyDefaultValuesFromExpectLowering.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableVersionOverloadsLowering | IR | K1+K2 | `ComposableVersionOverloadsLowering.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableDefaultParamLowering | IR | K1+K2 | `ComposableDefaultParamLowering.kt` |\n| compose | ComposerLambdaMemoization | IR | K1+K2 | `ComposerLambdaMemoization.kt` |\n| compose | ComposerParamTransformer | IR | K1+K2 | `ComposerParamTransformer.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableTargetAnnotationsTransformer | IR | K1+K2 | `ComposableTargetAnnotationsTransformer.kt` |\n| compose | ComposerIntrinsicTransformer | IR | K1+K2 | `ComposerIntrinsicTransformer.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableFunctionBodyTransformer | IR | K1+K2 | `ComposableFunctionBodyTransformer.kt` |\n| compose | KlibAssignableParamTransformer | IR | K1+K2 (non-JVM) | `KlibAssignableParamTransformer.kt` |\n| compose | WrapJsComposableLambdaLowering | IR | K1+K2 (JS/Wasm) | `WrapJsComposableLambdaLowering.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableCallChecker (K1) | - | K1 | `k1/ComposableCallChecker.kt` |\n| compose | ComposableDeclarationChecker (K1) | - | K1 | `k1/` |\n| compose | ComposableAnnotationChecker (K1) | - | K1 | `k1/` |\n| compose | ComposeDiagnosticSuppressor (K1) | - | K1 | `k1/` |\n| compose | ComposeTypeResolutionInterceptorExtension (K1) | - | K1 | `k1/` |\n\n### 各機能の詳細\n\n#### FIR Extensions (K2)\n\n##### ComposableFunctionTypeKindExtension\n- **継承/実装**: `FirFunctionTypeKindExtension(session)`\n- **オーバーライドメソッド**: `FunctionTypeKindRegistrar.registerKinds()`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - `ComposableFunction` と `KComposableFunction` の2つの FunctionTypeKind を登録\n  - `ComposableFunction`: `@Composable` アノテーション付き関数型を表現する。`isInlineable = true`\n  - `KComposableFunction`: reflect 版 (KFunction 相当)。`isInlineable = false`\n  - K1 互換性のため、`serializeAsFunctionWithAnnotationUntil` を設定 (アノテーション付き通常関数型としてシリアライズ)\n\n##### ComposeFirCheckersExtension\n- **継承/実装**: `FirAdditionalCheckersExtension(session)`\n- **登録チェッカー**:\n  - Declaration: `ComposableFunctionChecker`, `ComposablePropertyChecker`\n  - Type: `ComposableAnnotationChecker`\n  - Expression: `ComposableFunctionCallChecker`, `ComposableTargetChecker`, `ComposablePropertyAccessExpressionChecker`, `ComposablePropertyReferenceChecker`\n\n##### ComposableFunctionChecker\n- **継承/実装**: `FirFunctionChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common)`\n- **オーバーライドメソッド**: `check(declaration: FirFunction)`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - オーバーライド間で `@Composable` の不一致を `CONFLICTING_OVERLOADS` として報告\n  - `expect`/`actual` 間で `@Composable` の不一致を `MISMATCHED_COMPOSABLE_IN_EXPECT_ACTUAL` として報告\n  - `@Composable suspend fun` を `COMPOSABLE_SUSPEND_FUN` として報告\n  - open composable のデフォルトパラメータの互換性メタデータ不足を `DEPRECATED_OPEN_COMPOSABLE_DEFAULT_PARAMETER_VALUE` として警告\n  - abstract composable のデフォルトパラメータを `ABSTRACT_COMPOSABLE_DEFAULT_PARAMETER_VALUE` として報告\n  - open composable のデフォルトパラメータを `OPEN_COMPOSABLE_DEFAULT_PARAMETER_VALUE` として報告\n  - `@Composable fun main()` を `COMPOSABLE_FUN_MAIN` として報告\n  - `@Composable operator setValue` を `COMPOSE_INVALID_DELEGATE` として報告\n  - applier declaration の mismatch を `COMPOSE_APPLIER_DECLARATION_MISMATCH` として警告\n\n##### ComposablePropertyChecker\n- **継承/実装**: `FirPropertyChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common)`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - `@Composable var` を `COMPOSABLE_VAR` として報告\n  - backing field のある `@Composable` プロパティを `COMPOSABLE_PROPERTY_BACKING_FIELD` として報告\n\n##### ComposablePropertyReferenceChecker\n- **継承/実装**: `FirCallableReferenceAccessChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common)`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - delegate でない `@Composable` プロパティへの参照を `COMPOSABLE_PROPERTY_REFERENCE` として報告\n\n##### ComposableAnnotationChecker (Type)\n- **継承/実装**: `FirResolvedTypeRefChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common)`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - 関数型でない型に `@Composable` が付いている場合を `COMPOSABLE_INAPPLICABLE_TYPE` として報告\n\n##### ComposableFunctionCallChecker\n- **継承/実装**: `FirFunctionCallChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common)`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - composable 関数の呼び出しが composable コンテキスト内かチェック\n  - 非 composable 関数内での composable 呼び出し -> `COMPOSABLE_INVOCATION` + `COMPOSABLE_EXPECTED`\n  - `try` ブロック内での composable 呼び出し -> `ILLEGAL_TRY_CATCH_AROUND_COMPOSABLE`\n  - `runCatching` 内での composable 呼び出し -> `ILLEGAL_RUN_CATCHING_AROUND_COMPOSABLE`\n  - `@ReadOnlyComposable` 内での non-readonly 呼び出し -> `NONREADONLY_CALL_IN_READONLY_COMPOSABLE`\n  - `@DisallowComposableCalls` ラムダ内での composable 呼び出し -> `CAPTURED_COMPOSABLE_INVOCATION`\n  - `key()` 呼び出しの引数なし -> `KEY_CALL_WITH_NO_ARGUMENTS`\n  - inline ラムダの invoke で `@DisallowComposableCalls` なし -> `MISSING_DISALLOW_COMPOSABLE_CALLS_ANNOTATION`\n\n##### ComposableTargetChecker / ComposableTargetSessionStorage\n- **継承/実装**: `FirFunctionCallChecker(MppCheckerKind.Common)` / `FirExtensionSessionComponent(session)`\n- **動作の詳細**:\n  - `@ComposableTarget` / `@ComposableOpenTarget` アノテーションを使った applier 推論を行う\n  - 推論結果と宣言が矛盾する場合 -> `COMPOSE_APPLIER_CALL_MISMATCH`, `COMPOSE_APPLIER_PARAMETER_MISMATCH`\n  - `ComposableTargetSessionStorage` は推論のキャッシュ (LazyScheme, parent 関係, ノードキャッシュ) を管理\n\n#### IR Lowering パス (実行順序通り)\n\n##### 1. ComposableLambdaAnnotator (K2 only)\n- **継承/実装**: `IrVisitorVoid`\n- **動作**: K2 では composable ラムダの型が `ComposableFunction` だが、バックエンドは `@Composable` アノテーションを期待する。このパスが composable ラムダの `IrFunction` に `@Composable` アノテーションを追加する\n\n##### 2. AddHiddenFromObjCLowering (Native only)\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering` (implements `ModuleLoweringPass`)\n- **動作**: `@Composable` 型を含む関数/プロパティに `@HiddenFromObjC` アノテーションを追加。ObjC には composable 関数をエクスポートしない\n\n##### 3. ClassStabilityTransformer\n- **継承/実装**: `ClassLoweringPass` (implements `ModuleLoweringPass`)\n- **動作**: 全クラスの安定性 (Stability) を推論し、`@StabilityInferred` アノテーションと `static final int $stable` フィールドをクラスに追加。ランタイムがスキッピング判定に使用\n- **依存**: なし (最初期に実行)\n\n##### 4. LiveLiteralTransformer (オプション)\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering`\n- **動作**: リテラル値をランタイムで差し替え可能にする。リテラルを `liveLiteral(\"key\")` 呼び出しに変換し、State オブジェクトでラップ。Hot reload 用\n- **条件**: `liveLiteralsEnabled` または `liveLiteralsV2Enabled` が true の場合のみ\n\n##### 5. ComposableFunInterfaceLowering\n- **継承/実装**: `IrElementTransformerVoidWithContext` (implements `ModuleLoweringPass`)\n- **動作**: `@Composable` SAM 変換 (`fun interface` の SAM コンバージョン) を修正。JVM では `FunctionReferenceBuilder` でラッパークラスを生成、Native では `IrRichFunctionReference` を使用\n- **条件**: JVM または Native (+ IrRichCallableReferencesInKlibs) のみ\n\n##### 6. DurableFunctionKeyTransformer\n- **継承/実装**: `IrElementTransformerVoid` (implements `ModuleLoweringPass`)\n- **動作**: 各 composable 関数に対してソース位置ベースのハッシュキーを生成し `BindingTrace` に格納。後段パスが `startGroup(key)` 等で使用。オプションで `@FunctionKeyMeta` アノテーションも生成\n\n##### 7. CopyDefaultValuesFromExpectLowering (K1 only)\n- **継承/実装**: `IrElementTransformerVoid`\n- **動作**: `expect fun` の composable 関数のデフォルト値を `actual fun` にコピー。K2 では不要\n\n##### 8. ComposableVersionOverloadsLowering\n- **継承/実装**: `VersionOverloadsLowering`\n- **動作**: composable 関数の `@IntroducedAt` パラメータアノテーションを処理してバージョンオーバーロードを生成し、処理後にアノテーションを除去 (二重実行防止)\n\n##### 9. ComposableDefaultParamLowering\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering`\n- **動作**: abstract/open composable 関数のデフォルトパラメータを処理。`ComposeDefaultsImpl` ネストクラスを生成し、デフォルト値のプリアンブルを含む static ラッパーメソッドを配置。呼び出し元はこのラッパーを使用\n\n##### 10. ComposerLambdaMemoization\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering`\n- **動作**:\n  - composable ラムダを `composableLambda()` / `composableLambdaInstance()` でラップ\n  - 非 composable ラムダをメモ化 (`remember` 的な仕組み)\n  - キャプチャの安定性を分析し、安定キャプチャのみなら `composableLambdaInstance` (キャッシュ可能)\n  - StrongSkipping モード: 不安定なキャプチャがあっても特定条件でメモ化\n- **依存**: `ComposerParamTransformer` の前に実行\n\n##### 11. ComposerParamTransformer\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering`\n- **動作**: **最も重要な変換の一つ**。全ての composable 関数に `$composer: Composer` と `$changed: Int` (+ `$default: Int`) パラメータを追加。全ての呼び出しサイトも対応するパラメータを渡すように変換。型の再マッピングも行い、composable 関数型を正しい引数数の関数型に変換\n\n##### 12. ComposableTargetAnnotationsTransformer\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering`\n- **動作**: FIR で推論された applier target 情報を IR アノテーション (`@ComposableTarget`, `@ComposableOpenTarget`, `@ComposableInferredTarget`) として書き出す\n\n##### 13. ComposerIntrinsicTransformer\n- **継承/実装**: `IrElementTransformerVoid` (implements `FileLoweringPass`, `ModuleLoweringPass`)\n- **動作**: `currentComposer` の呼び出しを、`ComposerParamTransformer` で追加された `$composer` パラメータへの参照に置き換える\n- **依存**: `ComposerParamTransformer` の後に実行\n\n##### 14. ComposableFunctionBodyTransformer\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering` (implements `FileLoweringPass`)\n- **動作**: **最大かつ最も複雑な変換**。composable 関数の本体を以下のように変換:\n  - `startRestartGroup()` / `endRestartGroup()` の挿入\n  - `$changed` パラメータを使ったスキッピングロジックの生成\n  - `if (changed and 0bXXX == 0)` 形式の changed ビットチェック\n  - `startReplaceGroup` / `startMovableGroup` / `startDefaults` 等の group 管理\n  - `remember` のイントリンシック最適化 (IntrinsicRemember)\n  - NonSkippingGroup 最適化\n  - PausableComposition 対応\n  - `$default` マスクを使ったデフォルト値の条件分岐\n- **依存**: `ComposerParamTransformer` と `ComposerIntrinsicTransformer` の後\n\n##### 15. KlibAssignableParamTransformer (non-JVM only)\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering`\n- **動作**: KT-44945 の回避策。`$composer` パラメータへの再代入 (`$composer = $composer.startRestartGroup(...)`) を、ローカル変数への置き換えで実現\n- **条件**: non-JVM (klib) ターゲットのみ\n\n##### 16. WrapJsComposableLambdaLowering (JS/Wasm only)\n- **継承/実装**: `AbstractComposeLowering`\n- **動作**: JS/Wasm で `composableLambda` が `ComposableLambda` インスタンスを返すが、これは FunctionX インターフェースを実装しない。そのため、呼び出しサイトを `invoke` 呼び出しでラップし、正しく動作するようにする\n- **条件**: JS または Wasm ターゲットのみ\n\n#### IR パスの依存関係まとめ\n\n```\nComposableLambdaAnnotator (K2 only, 最初)\n    |\nAddHiddenFromObjCLowering (Native only)\n    |\nClassStabilityTransformer (全プラットフォーム)\n    |\nLiveLiteralTransformer (オプション)\n    |\nComposableFunInterfaceLowering (JVM/Native)\n    |\nDurableFunctionKeyTransformer\n    |\nCopyDefaultValuesFromExpectLowering (K1 only)\n    |\nComposableVersionOverloadsLowering\n    |\nComposableDefaultParamLowering\n    |\nComposerLambdaMemoization  <-- ラムダのラップ (ComposerParam の前)\n    |\nComposerParamTransformer    <-- $composer/$changed 追加 (全 composable 関数)\n    |\nComposableTargetAnnotationsTransformer\n    |\nComposerIntrinsicTransformer <-- currentComposer -> $composer 置換\n    |\nComposableFunctionBodyTransformer <-- 関数本体の変換 (group, skipping)\n    |\nKlibAssignableParamTransformer (non-JVM)\n    |\nWrapJsComposableLambdaLowering (JS/Wasm)\n```\n\n### ComposeErrors 診断メッセージ一覧\n\n| 診断名 | 種別 | 内容 |\n|---|---|---|\n| `COMPOSABLE_INVOCATION` | error | 非 composable 関数内での composable 呼び出し (呼び出し側) |\n| `COMPOSABLE_EXPECTED` | error | composable 呼び出しを含む非 composable 関数 (宣言側) |\n| `NONREADONLY_CALL_IN_READONLY_COMPOSABLE` | error | ReadOnlyComposable 内での non-readonly 呼び出し |\n| `CAPTURED_COMPOSABLE_INVOCATION` | error | @DisallowComposableCalls ラムダ内での composable 呼び出し |\n| `ILLEGAL_TRY_CATCH_AROUND_COMPOSABLE` | error | try ブロック内での composable 呼び出し |\n| `ILLEGAL_RUN_CATCHING_AROUND_COMPOSABLE` | error | runCatching 内での composable 呼び出し |\n| `MISSING_DISALLOW_COMPOSABLE_CALLS_ANNOTATION` | error | inline ラムダパラメータに @DisallowComposableCalls がない |\n| `COMPOSABLE_SUSPEND_FUN` | error | @Composable suspend fun は不可 |\n| `COMPOSABLE_FUN_MAIN` | error | @Composable main 関数は不可 |\n| `COMPOSABLE_VAR` | error | @Composable var プロパティは不可 |\n| `COMPOSABLE_PROPERTY_BACKING_FIELD` | error | backing field 付き @Composable プロパティは不可 |\n|
